summary-field-show-more"" dir=""ltr"">PRÜFTECHNIK, headquartered in Ismaning, near Munich, Germany. Our core business areas are high-tech measuring systems for industrial maintenance and quality assurance Covering Condition Monitoring (CM), Laser Alignment Systems (ALI) and NDT.<br/><br/>
PRÜFTECHNIK was founded in 1972 by Dieter Busch. The early international orientation of the company proved to be crucial to the further growth of our business. With 20 operational sales, service, development and production locations, and exports to over 70 countries, PRÜFTECHNIK has evolved into a successful global player.<br/><br/>
PRÜFTECHNIK is the global leader in shaft alignment systems. Our award-winning alignment products have become standard equipment in many industry sectors. Innovative machine monitoring systems for all machine types and sizes serve our customers to optimize system availability and enable a high level of productivity. Inspection systems for the nondestructive testing of semi-finished products are integrated in the production process to assure high product quality. We keep in close touch with our customers by offering not only precision instruments but a range of high-end maintenance services.<br/><br/>
